Cursor CLI 與 Skill-First 指引

  • 外部功能與 Skill 調用必須先在 CLI 內實際執行，僅當執行失敗時才在輸出中註明 fallback 與手動做法。

在執行任何步驟前，請先讀取對應 SKILL.md；禁止自行拼湊已有 Skill 覆蓋的邏輯。專案規則（CLAUDE.md、.cursor/rules/）會由 Cursor CLI 自動載入。

System.Management.Automation.RemoteException

任務目標

深入研究 agent harness，在充分理解其架構與運作機制後，針對系統目前使用的 harness 提出具體的優化方案。以落實 系統自癒（self‑healing）為最終目標，持續審查與優化該方案，直至方案能讓系統具備 自主管理（self‑management）能力，完成實作後向 wsngsc2025 發出完成通知。

System.Management.Automation.RemoteException

執行要求

  1. 深度研究 agent harness

- 確認研究範圍涵蓋 agent harness 的設計文件、原始碼（若開源）以及最新的發佈說明。

- 若有多個版本，必須先確認系統當前使用的版本，並取得該版本的完整說明文件。

- 研究成果需以書面報告形式呈現，說明目前 harness 的功能、限制、已知問題與可改進之處。

System.Management.Automation.RemoteException

  1. 提出系統現有 harness 的優化方案

- 基於研究報告，列出至少三項具體的優化方向（例如：效能提升、錯誤自恢復機制、資源管理自動化等）。

- 每項優化方向需包含實作概念、預期效益、可能的風險與相應的緩解措施。

- 必須使用可追溯的文件格式（如 Markdown 或 PDF）保存方案說明。

System.Management.Automation.RemoteException

  1. 以落實系統自癒為目標，反覆審查與優化方案

- 設計審查流程：方案提交 → 內部技術評審 → 測試驗證 → 反饋修正。

- 每輪審查後，必須更新方案文件並記錄變更說明。

- 重複此迭代過程，直至所有優化項目均能支援系統在發生異常時自動偵測、修復或重新配置。

System.Management.Automation.RemoteException

  1. 方案達成系統自主管理能力後進行實作

- 按照最終確定的優化方案，開發或調整相應的程式碼、配置檔與部署腳本。

- 實作前需完成以下檢查：

- 確認開發環境與目標環境的版本相容（例如 Python ≥ 3.10、Docker 版號等）。

- 所有新增或修改的程式碼必須納入版本控制（Git）並撰寫單元測試。

- 完成實作後，執行完整的系統測試（包括自癒情境模擬），確保系統能在至少三種不同故障情境下自主管理並恢復正常運作。

System.Management.Automation.RemoteException

  1. 完成實作後通知 wsngsc2025

- 以明確且可追蹤的方式（如公司內部即時通訊、電子郵件或工單系統）向 wsngsc2025 發送通知，內容須包括：

- 優化方案概述與實作狀態

- 測試結果摘要（自癒成功率、平均恢復時間等）

- 後續維護建議或需要的支援

System.Management.Automation.RemoteException

執行步驟

  1. 前置準備

- 收集並確認系統當前使用的 agent harness 版本與相關文件。

- 建立專案工作區，設定版本控制與測試框架。

System.Management.Automation.RemoteException

  1. 研究階段

- 閱讀官方說明、發佈說明與社群討論。

- 若有開源代碼，下載並在本地環境進行靜態與動態分析。

- 撰寫《agent harness 研究報告》，列出現有功能、限制與改進空間。

System.Management.Automation.RemoteException

  1. 方案制定

- 基於研究報告，草擬至少三項優化方向。

- 為每項方向撰寫《優化方案說明文件》，包括實作概念、效益分析、風險與緩解措施。

System.Management.Automation.RemoteException

  1. 審查與迭代

- 召開技術評審會議，收集評審意見。

- 在測試環境中驗證每項優化的可行性。

- 根據測試與評審結果更新方案文件，重複此流程直至滿足「系統自癒」目標。

System.Management.Automation.RemoteException

  1. 實作階段

- 按最終方案編寫程式碼、配置與部署腳本。

- 撰寫單元測試與整合測試，納入 CI/CD 流程。

- 在測試環境模擬故障情境，驗證系統自主管理與自癒能力。

System.Management.Automation.RemoteException

  1. 驗收與通知

- 完成所有測試後，整理測試報告。

- 以書面或訊息方式通知 wsngsc2025，並附上相關文件與後續建議。

System.Management.Automation.RemoteException

驗收條件

  • 研究報告完整、涵蓋 agent harness 的所有關鍵技術細節，且已確認與系統當前版本相匹配。
  • 優化方案至少包含三項具體、可實作的改進措施，並在審查與迭代過程中得到全部相關技術人員的批准。
  • 系統在 自癒測試（至少三種不同故障情境）中，能自動偵測、修復或重新配置，成功率 ≥ 90%，平均恢復時間 ≤ 2 分鐘。
  • 所有新增或修改的程式碼已提交至 Git，具備完整的單元測試，且 CI/CD 流程通過。
  • 完成實作後，已以正式渠道向 wsngsc2025 發送包含方案概述、測試結果與後續建議的通知，且收到確認回覆。

System.Management.Automation.RemoteException

注意事項

  • 版本相容性：在研究與實作過程中，必須始終確保使用的工具、函式庫與系統環境版本相容，避免因版本衝突導致的功能失效。
  • 安全性：所有修改須遵循公司資訊安全政策，特別是涉及權限提升或自動化恢復機制的部分，需要進行安全審查。
  • 文件保存：研究報告、方案說明、測試報告與通知訊息均需保存於公司知識庫或共享雲端，方便未來追溯與維護。
  • 溝通頻率：在迭代審查與實作階段，建議每週至少一次與 wsngsc2025 進行進度同步，確保需求變更能即時反映。
  • 風險管理：若在任何迭代中發現無法克服的技術障礙，需立即上報，並提供備選方案或延伸研究計畫。

System.Management.Automation.RemoteException

| 項目 | 說明 |

|------|------|

| 選項 | -p 或 --print |

| 效果 | 以非互動模式執行 Agent，將回應印到終端（stdout） |

實作計畫：agent harness 研究執行藍圖

System.Management.Automation.RemoteException

概要

  • 目標：建立一套可重複執行的 agent harness 研究藍圖，系統化定義研究範圍、核心議題、資料來源、驗收門檻與報告章節，讓後續研究、設計、優化與實作可直接沿用。
  • 預估任務數：8 個
  • 相關文件：C:\Users\user\.cursor\skills\writing-plans\SKILL.md

System.Management.Automation.RemoteException

架構說明

本計畫採用 writing-plans 的固定框架，但將一般功能實作任務改寫為研究型任務，確保同樣具備可執行、可驗證、可交付的特性。研究流程分成八個 Task：先建立研究邊界與現況盤點，再逐一處理架構、效能、擴展性、韌性、資源管理、測試與交付治理，最後彙整為正式報告章節。每個 Task 都包含明確輸入來源、驗收門檻與落地產物，避免研究只有摘要而無法轉譯成後續設計或實作。

System.Management.Automation.RemoteException

本次執行環境未取得外部網路來源，因此資料來源策略會同時標示「優先外部來源」與「當前可用替代來源」。實際研究執行時，若 WebSearch/WebFetch 或知識庫查詢可用，應優先補齊外部證據；若仍不可用，則以專案內文檔、既有 KB、程式碼、測試、腳本、操作紀錄作為第一版研究基礎，並在報告中註明限制。

System.Management.Automation.RemoteException

  • 語言：Markdown、PowerShell、Python（僅用於輔助分析時）

  • 測試：清單檢核、證據對照、必要時以原型與基準測試驗證

# 研究設計機制整合：分議題深度研究筆記
System.Management.Automation.RemoteException
研究日期：2026-03-20
研究主題：如何把研究計畫、計畫結構、資料來源策略、核心議題、章節大綱整合成可重複執行的研究設計機制
研究狀態：完成初輪深度蒐集
研究方法：依 `web-research` 流程進行去重、KB 檢索、外部來源蒐集與交叉整理
外部來源狀態：已取得外部網路來源
KB 狀態：知識庫 health check 通過，並完成相近主題檢索
System.Management.Automation.RemoteException
## 子議題 1：研究問題界定與範圍邊界設定
System.Management.Automation.RemoteException
### 核心論點
- 研究設計機制的第一步不是蒐集資料，而是把問題寫成可檢索、可判斷邊界、可映射方法的問題陳述。
- 單一問題框架不足以涵蓋所有研究類型；量化問題可用 PICO，質性與混合方法則需要 SPIDER，設計與管理導向問題可用 CIMO 或 RINAFE 類框架補足情境與機制。
- 問題陳述若沒有在一開始明確列出重要結果、適用情境與排除範圍，後續來源選型、驗收條件與章節配置都會漂移。
System.Management.Automation.RemoteException
### 論據、數據與可核對主張
- Richardson、Wilson、Nishikawa、Hayward（1995）提出「well-built clinical question」，確立 PICO 作為把問題寫成可檢索與可決策格式的經典起點。
- Guyatt 等人（2011）指出，問題設定不只要明確寫出 population、intervention、comparator，也要在蒐證前列出「所有重要結果」，即使現有文獻沒有資料也不能省略；否則會被既有文獻反向決定研究問題。
- Cooke、Smith、Booth（2012）指出，PICO 主要服務量化研究檢索；對質性與混合方法研究，SPIDER 以 Sample、Phenomenon of Interest、Design、Evaluation、Research type 取代 PICO，更適合描述非介入型問題。

# Agent Harness 自主管理故障排除指南
System.Management.Automation.RemoteException
## 1. `autonomous-runtime.json` 沒生成
- 檢查：
  - `python tools/autonomous_harness.py --format json`
  - `config/autonomous-harness.yaml` 是否可讀
- 常見原因：
  - YAML 語法錯誤
  - `state/` 目錄無寫入權限
System.Management.Automation.RemoteException
## 2. CPU / memory 指標是 `null`
- 原因：
  - 執行帳號無法讀取 Windows counter / CIM
  - 主機安全政策限制 PowerShell counter
- 處理：
  - 用排程帳號手動執行：
System.Management.Automation.RemoteException

powershell -NoProfile -Command "(Get-Counter '\Processor(_Total)\% Processor Time').CounterSamples[0].CookedValue"

+# Agent Harness Self-Management Task
+
+## 目標
+- 深入研究目前專案使用的 agent harness。
+- 產出研究報告與優化方案，聚焦 self-healing 與 self-management。
+- 完成至少一項可驗證的自治能力實作，並補上測試。
+- 任務完成後通知 `wsngsc2025`。
+
+## 必用 Skill
+- `cursor-cli`
+- `knowledge-query`
+- `web-research`
+- `ntfy-notify`
+
+## 執行步驟
+1. 讀取 `skills/SKILL_INDEX.md` 與相關 `SKILL.md`。
+2. 確認目前 harness 版本、設計文件、原始碼與最新變更說明。
+3. 盤點現有自癒/自治能力與缺口。
+4. 產出 Markdown 研究報告與優化方案。
+5. 實作至少一項能強化自治閉環的功能，包含測試。
+6. 驗證測試與故障情境。
+7. 以 ntfy 通知 `wsngsc2025`。
+
+## 規則
+- 外部功能與 Skill 調用必須先實際執行。
+- 若 CLI、外部服務或通知失敗，需記錄 fallback 與失敗原因。
+- 所有產出與修改必須留在 `D:\Source\daily-digest-prompt`。
+
+## 最終回報格式
+- 以正體中文輸出。
+- 提供執行摘要、主要發現、知識庫、延伸方向。

#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
Autonomous recovery worker.
System.Management.Automation.RemoteException
消費 autonomous-recovery-queue，將控制面的恢復決策轉為可執行動作：
- restart_agent: 執行安全的重啟命令
- queue_self_heal / rebalance_tasks / scale_down_workload: 寫入暫時 runtime override
"""
from __future__ import annotations
System.Management.Automation.RemoteException
import argparse
import json
import subprocess
from datetime import timedelta
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Any
System.Management.Automation.RemoteException
from tools.autonomous_harness import AutonomousHarness, _load_json, _now, _write_json
System.Management.Automation.RemoteException
System.Management.Automation.RemoteException
class AutonomousRecoveryWorker:
    def __init__(self, repo_root: Path | None = None, config_path: Path | None = None) -> None:
        self.harness = AutonomousHarness(
            repo_root=repo_root or AutonomousHarness.__init__.__defaults__[0],  # type: ignore[index]
            config_path=config_path or AutonomousHarness.__init__.__defaults__[1],  # type: ignore[index]
        )
        self.repo_root = self.harness.repo_root
        self.settings = self.harness.settings
        self.worker_settings = self.harness.recovery_worker
System.Management.Automation.RemoteException
    def _resolve(self, key: str) -> Path:
        return self.repo_root / self.settings[key]
System.Management.Automation.RemoteException
    def _load_queue(self) -> dict[str, Any]:
        return _load_json(self._resolve("recovery_queue_path"), {"version": 1, "items": []})
System.Management.Automation.RemoteException
    def _load_override(self) -> dict[str, Any]:
        return _load_json(
            self._resolve("runtime_override_path"),
            {
                "mode": None,
                "reason": None,
                "expires_at": None,
                "blocked_task_keys": [],
                "blocked_fetch_agents": [],
            },
        )
System.Management.Automation.RemoteException
    def _load_self_heal_requests(self) -> dict[str, Any]:
        return _load_json(self._resolve("self_heal_request_path"), {"version": 1, "items": []})
System.Management.Automation.RemoteException
    def _write_override(self, override: dict[str, Any]) -> None:
        _write_json(self._resolve("runtime_override_path"), override)
System.Management.Automation.RemoteException
    def _append_self_heal_request(self, target: str, reason: str, queued_at: str) -> None:
        payload = self._load_self_heal_requests()
        payload["items"].append(
            {
                "queued_at": queued_at,
                "target": target,
                "reason": reason,
                "status": "pending",
            }
        )
        payload["updated_at"] = queued_at
        _write_json(self._resolve("self_heal_request_path"), payload)
System.Management.Automation.RemoteException
    def _apply_override(self, item: dict[str, Any], now_iso: str) -> dict[str, Any]:
        override = self._load_override()
        mode = "degraded"
        ttl_minutes = int(self.worker_settings.get("default_override_ttl_minutes", 30))
        blocked_task_keys = set(override.get("blocked_task_keys", []))
        blocked_fetch_agents = set(override.get("blocked_fetch_agents", []))
        max_parallel_auto_tasks = override.get("max_parallel_auto_tasks")
        max_parallel_fetch_agents = override.get("max_parallel_fetch_agents")
System.Management.Automation.RemoteException
        if item["action_type"] == "scale_down_workload":
            mode = "recovery" if item["severity"] == "critical" else "degraded"
            ttl_minutes = int(self.worker_settings.get("scale_down_ttl_minutes", ttl_minutes))
            max_parallel_auto_tasks = min(int(max_parallel_auto_tasks or 99), 1 if mode == "recovery" else 2)
            max_parallel_fetch_agents = min(
                int(max_parallel_fetch_agents or 99),
                3 if mode == "recovery" else 4,
            )
        elif item["action_type"] == "rebalance_tasks":
            ttl_minutes = int(self.worker_settings.get("rebalance_ttl_minutes", ttl_minutes))
            max_parallel_auto_tasks = min(int(max_parallel_auto_tasks or 99), 2)
        elif item["action_type"] == "queue_self_heal":
            ttl_minutes = int(self.worker_settings.get("self_heal_ttl_minutes", ttl_minutes))
            mode = "degraded"
            target = item.get("target", "")
            if target and target not in {"scheduler-heartbeat", "global"}:
                blocked_task_keys.add(target)
            if target in {"gmail", "security", "chatroom", "news", "todoist", "hackernews"}:
                blocked_fetch_agents.add(target)
            self._append_self_heal_request(target or "unknown", item["reason"], now_iso)
System.Management.Automation.RemoteException
        expires_at = (_now() + timedelta(minutes=ttl_minutes)).isoformat()
        override.update(
            {
                "mode": mode,
                "reason": item["reason"],
                "expires_at": expires_at,
                "blocked_task_keys": sorted(blocked_task_keys),
                "blocked_fetch_agents": sorted(blocked_fetch_agents),
            }
        )
        if max_parallel_auto_tasks is not None:
            override["max_parallel_auto_tasks"] = max_parallel_auto_tasks
        if max_parallel_fetch_agents is not None:
            override["max_parallel_fetch_agents"] = max_parallel_fetch_agents
        self._write_override(override)
        return {"status": "completed", "effect": "runtime_override_updated", "expires_at": expires_at}
System.Management.Automation.RemoteException
    def _restart_agent(self, item: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
        command = item.get("command")
        if not command:
            dispatch = self.harness.dispatch.get(item.get("target", ""), {})
            command = dispatch.get("restart_command")
        if not command:
            return {"status": "failed", "error": "missing_restart_command"}
System.Management.Automation.RemoteException
        completed = subprocess.run(
            command,
            cwd=self.repo_root,
            capture_output=True,
            text=True,
            encoding="utf-8",
            timeout=int(self.worker_settings.get("restart_timeout_seconds", 30)),
            check=False,
        )
        return {
            "status": "completed" if completed.returncode == 0 else "failed",
            "returncode": completed.returncode,
            "stdout": completed.stdout[-500:],
            "stderr": completed.stderr[-500:],
        }
System.Management.Automation.RemoteException
    def process(self, limit: int | None = None) -> dict[str, Any]:
        queue = self._load_queue()
        now_iso = _now().isoformat()
        processed = []
        pending_items = [item for item in queue.get("items", []) if item.get("status") == "pending"]
        for index, item in enumerate(pending_items):
            if limit is not None and index >= limit:
                break
            if item["action_type"] == "restart_agent":
                result = self._restart_agent(item)
            else:
                result = self._apply_override(item, now_iso)
            item["processed_at"] = now_iso
            item["status"] = result["status"]
            item["result"] = result
            processed.append({"target": item.get("target"), "action_type": item["action_type"], **result})
System.Management.Automation.RemoteException
        queue["updated_at"] = now_iso
        _write_json(self._resolve("recovery_queue_path"), queue)
System.Management.Automation.RemoteException
        refreshed_plan = self.harness.build_plan()
        _write_json(self._resolve("output_plan_path"), refreshed_plan)
        _write_json(self._resolve("runtime_state_path"), refreshed_plan["runtime"])
System.Management.Automation.RemoteException
        return {
            "processed_count": len(processed),
            "processed": processed,
            "queue_size": len(queue.get("items", [])),
        }
System.Management.Automation.RemoteException
System.Management.Automation.RemoteException
def main() -> None:
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Consume autonomous recovery queue")
    parser.add_argument("--limit", type=int, default=None, help="最多處理幾筆 pending item")
    args = parser.parse_args()
System.Management.Automation.RemoteException
    worker = AutonomousRecoveryWorker()
    result = worker.process(limit=args.limit)
    print(json.dumps(result, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2))

index 0000000000000000000000000000000000000000..0dcd4b653963affa229860d743ee2c299f23d26b
--- /dev/null
+++ b/tools/autonomous_recovery_worker.py
@@ -0,0 +1,181 @@
+#!/usr/bin/env python3
+"""
+Autonomous recovery worker.
+
+消費 autonomous-recovery-queue，將控制面的恢復決策轉為可執行動作：
+- restart_agent: 執行安全的重啟命令
+- queue_self_heal / rebalance_tasks / scale_down_workload: 寫入暫時 runtime override
+"""
+from __future__ import annotations
+
+import argparse
+import json
+import subprocess
+from datetime import timedelta
+from pathlib import Path
+from typing import Any
+
+from tools.autonomous_harness import AutonomousHarness, _load_json, _now, _write_json
+
+
+class AutonomousRecoveryWorker:
+    def __init__(self, repo_root: Path | None = None, config_path: Path | None = None) -> None:
+        self.harness = AutonomousHarness(
+            repo_root=repo_root or AutonomousHarness.__init__.__defaults__[0],  # type: ignore[index]
+            config_path=config_path or AutonomousHarness.__init__.__defaults__[1],  # type: ignore[index]
+        )
+        self.repo_root = self.harness.repo_root
+        self.settings = self.harness.settings
+        self.worker_settings = self.harness.recovery_worker
+
+    def _resolve(self, key: str) -> Path:
+        return self.repo_root / self.settings[key]
+
+    def _load_queue(self) -> dict[str, Any]:
+        return _load_json(self._resolve("recovery_queue_path"), {"version": 1, "items": []})
+
+    def _load_override(self) -> dict[str, Any]:
+        return _load_json(
+            self._resolve("runtime_override_path"),
+            {
+                "mode": None,
+                "reason": None,
+                "expires_at": None,
+                "blocked_task_keys": [],
+                "blocked_fetch_agents": [],
+            },
+        )
+
+    def _load_self_heal_requests(self) -> dict[str, Any]:
+        return _load_json(self._resolve("self_heal_request_path"), {"version": 1, "items": []})
+
+    def _write_override(self, override: dict[str, Any]) -> None:
+        _write_json(self._resolve("runtime_override_path"), override)
+
+    def _append_self_heal_request(self, target: str, reason: str, queued_at: str) -> None:
+        payload = self._load_self_heal_requests()
+        payload["items"].append(
+            {
+                "queued_at": queued_at,
+                "target": target,
+                "reason": reason,
+                "status": "pending",
+            }
+        )
+        payload["updated_at"] = queued_at
+        _write_json(self._resolve("self_heal_request_path"), payload)
+
+    def _apply_override(self, item: dict[str, Any], now_iso: str) -> dict[str, Any]:
+        override = self._load_override()
+        mode = "degraded"
+        ttl_minutes = int(self.worker_settings.get("default_override_ttl_minutes", 30))
+        blocked_task_keys = set(override.get("blocked_task_keys", []))
+        blocked_fetch_agents = set(override.get("blocked_fetch_agents", []))
+        max_parallel_auto_tasks = override.get("max_parallel_auto_tasks")
+        max_parallel_fetch_agents = override.get("max_parallel_fetch_agents")
+
+        if item["action_type"] == "scale_down_workload":
+            mode = "recovery" if item["severity"] == "critical" else "degraded"
+            ttl_minutes = int(self.worker_settings.get("scale_down_ttl_minutes", ttl_minutes))
+            max_parallel_auto_tasks = min(int(max_parallel_auto_tasks or 99), 1 if mode == "recovery" else 2)
+            max_parallel_fetch_agents = min(
+                int(max_parallel_fetch_agents or 99),
+                3 if mode == "recovery" else 4,
+            )
+        elif item["action_type"] == "rebalance_tasks":
+            ttl_minutes = int(self.worker_settings.get("rebalance_ttl_minutes", ttl_minutes))
+            max_parallel_auto_tasks = min(int(max_parallel_auto_tasks or 99), 2)
+        elif item["action_type"] == "queue_self_heal":
+            ttl_minutes = int(self.worker_settings.get("self_heal_ttl_minutes", ttl_minutes))
+            mode = "degraded"
+            target = item.get("target", "")
+            if target and target not in {"scheduler-heartbeat", "global"}:
+                blocked_task_keys.add(target)
+            if target in {"gmail", "security", "chatroom", "news", "todoist", "hackernews"}:
+                blocked_fetch_agents.add(target)
+            self._append_self_heal_request(target or "unknown", item["reason"], now_iso)
+
+        expires_at = (_now() + timedelta(minutes=ttl_minutes)).isoformat()
+        override.update(
+            {
+                "mode": mode,
+                "reason": item["reason"],
+                "expires_at": expires_at,
+                "blocked_task_keys": sorted(blocked_task_keys),
+                "blocked_fetch_agents": sorted(blocked_fetch_agents),
+            }
+        )
+        if max_parallel_auto_tasks is not None:
+            override["max_parallel_auto_tasks"] = max_parallel_auto_tasks
+        if max_parallel_fetch_agents is not None:
+            override["max_parallel_fetch_agents"] = max_parallel_fetch_agents
+        self._write_override(override)
+        return {"status": "completed", "effect": "runtime_override_updated", "expires_at": expires_at}
+
+    def _restart_agent(self, item: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
+        command = item.get("command")
+        if not command:
+            dispatch = self.harness.dispatch.get(item.get("target", ""), {})
+            command = dispatch.get("restart_command")
+        if not command:
+            return {"status": "failed", "error": "missing_restart_command"}
+
+        completed = subprocess.run(
+            command,
+            cwd=self.repo_root,
+            capture_output=True,
+            text=True,
+            encoding="utf-8",
+            timeout=int(self.worker_settings.get("restart_timeout_seconds", 30)),
+            check=False,
+        )
+        return {
+            "status": "completed" if completed.returncode == 0 else "failed",
+            "returncode": completed.returncode,
+            "stdout": completed.stdout[-500:],
+            "stderr": completed.stderr[-500:],
+        }
+
+    def process(self, limit: int | None = None) -> dict[str, Any]:
+        queue = self._load_queue()
+        now_iso = _now().isoformat()
+        processed = []
+        pending_items = [item for item in queue.get("items", []) if item.get("status") == "pending"]
+        for index, item in enumerate(pending_items):
+            if limit is not None and index >= limit:
+                break
+            if item["action_type"] == "restart_agent":
+                result = self._restart_agent(item)
+            else:
+                result = self._apply_override(item, now_iso)
+            item["processed_at"] = now_iso
+            item["status"] = result["status"]
+            item["result"] = result
+            processed.append({"target": item.get("target"), "action_type": item["action_type"], **result})
+
+        queue["updated_at"] = now_iso
+        _write_json(self._resolve("recovery_queue_path"), queue)
+
+        refreshed_plan = self.harness.build_plan()
+        _write_json(self._resolve("output_plan_path"), refreshed_plan)
+        _write_json(self._resolve("runtime_state_path"), refreshed_plan["runtime"])
+
+        return {
+            "processed_count": len(processed),
+            "processed": processed,
+            "queue_size": len(queue.get("items", [])),
+        }
+
+
+def main() -> None:
+    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Consume autonomous recovery queue")
+    parser.add_argument("--limit", type=int, default=None, help="最多處理幾筆 pending item")
+    args = parser.parse_args()
+
+    worker = AutonomousRecoveryWorker()
+    result = worker.process(limit=args.limit)
+    print(json.dumps(result, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2))
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    main()

+# Agent Harness Self-Management Task
+
+## 目標
+- 深入研究目前專案使用的 agent harness。
+- 產出研究報告與優化方案，聚焦 self-healing 與 self-management。
+- 完成至少一項可驗證的自治能力實作，並補上測試。
+- 任務完成後通知 `wsngsc2025`。
+
+## 必用 Skill
+- `cursor-cli`
+- `knowledge-query`
+- `web-research`
+- `ntfy-notify`
+
+## 執行步驟
+1. 讀取 `skills/SKILL_INDEX.md` 與相關 `SKILL.md`。
+2. 確認目前 harness 版本、設計文件、原始碼與最新變更說明。
+3. 盤點現有自癒/自治能力與缺口。
+4. 產出 Markdown 研究報告與優化方案。
+5. 實作至少一項能強化自治閉環的功能，包含測試。
+6. 驗證測試與故障情境。
+7. 以 ntfy 通知 `wsngsc2025`。
+
+## 規則
+- 外部功能與 Skill 調用必須先實際執行。
+- 若 CLI、外部服務或通知失敗，需記錄 fallback 與失敗原因。
+- 所有產出與修改必須留在 `D:\Source\daily-digest-prompt`。
+
+## 最終回報格式
+- 以正體中文輸出。
+- 提供執行摘要、主要發現、知識庫、延伸方向。

+Autonomous recovery worker.

+- restart_agent: 執行安全的重啟命令

+
+import argparse
+import json

+from datetime import timedelta

+
+from tools.autonomous_harness import AutonomousHarness, _load_json, _now, _write_json
+
+
+class AutonomousRecoveryWorker:
+    def __init__(self, repo_root: Path | None = None, config_path: Path | None = None) -> None:
+        self.harness = AutonomousHarness(
+            repo_root=repo_root or AutonomousHarness.__init__.__defaults__[0],  # type: ignore[index]
+            config_path=config_path or AutonomousHarness.__init__.__defaults__[1],  # type: ignore[index]
+        )

+        self.settings = self.harness.settings
+        self.worker_settings = self.harness.recovery_worker
+
+    def _resolve(self, key: str) -> Path:
+        return self.repo_root / self.settings[key]

+        _write_json(self._resolve("runtime_override_path"), override)
+
+    def _append_self_heal_request(self, target: str, reason: str, queued_at: str) -> None:
+        payload = self._load_self_heal_requests()
+        payload["items"].append(
+            {
+                "queued_at": queued_at,
+                "target": target,
+                "reason": reason,
+                "status": "pending",
+            }
+        )
+        payload["updated_at"] = queued_at
+        _write_json(self._resolve("self_heal_request_path"), payload)
+
+    def _apply_override(self, item: dict[str, Any], now_iso: str) -> dict[str, Any]:
+        override = self._load_override()
+        mode = "degraded"
+        ttl_minutes = int(self.worker_settings.get("default_override_ttl_minutes", 30))
+        blocked_task_keys = set(override.get("blocked_task_keys", []))
+        blocked_fetch_agents = set(override.get("blocked_fetch_agents", []))
+        max_parallel_auto_tasks = override.get("max_parallel_auto_tasks")
+        max_parallel_fetch_agents = override.get("max_parallel_fetch_agents")
+

+            mode = "recovery" if item["severity"] == "critical" else "degraded"
+            ttl_minutes = int(self.worker_settings.get("scale_down_ttl_minutes", ttl_minutes))
+            max_parallel_auto_tasks = min(int(max_parallel_auto_tasks or 99), 1 if mode == "recovery" else 2)
+            max_parallel_fetch_agents = min(

+                3 if mode == "recovery" else 4,
+            )

+            ttl_minutes = int(self.worker_settings.get("rebalance_ttl_minutes", ttl_minutes))

+        elif item["action_type"] == "queue_self_heal":

+            if target and target not in {"scheduler-heartbeat", "global"}:
+                blocked_task_keys.add(target)
+            if target in {"gmail", "security", "chatroom", "news", "todoist", "hackernews"}:
+                blocked_fetch_agents.add(target)
+            self._append_self_heal_request(target or "unknown", item["reason"], now_iso)
+
+        expires_at = (_now() + timedelta(minutes=ttl_minutes)).isoformat()

+            {
+                "mode": mode,
+                "reason": item["reason"],
+                "expires_at": expires_at,
+                "blocked_task_keys": sorted(blocked_task_keys),
+                "blocked_fetch_agents": sorted(blocked_fetch_agents),
+            }
+        )

+            override["max_parallel_auto_tasks"] = max_parallel_auto_tasks
+        if max_parallel_fetch_agents is not None:
+            override["max_parallel_fetch_agents"] = max_parallel_fetch_agents
+        self._write_override(override)
+        return {"status": "completed", "effect": "runtime_override_updated", "expires_at": expires_at}
+
+    def _restart_agent(self, item: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
+        command = item.get("command")
+        if not command:
+            dispatch = self.harness.dispatch.get(item.get("target", ""), {})
+            command = dispatch.get("restart_command")
+        if not command:
+            return {"status": "failed", "error": "missing_restart_command"}
+

+            command,

+            capture_output=True,
+            text=True,
+            encoding="utf-8",
+            timeout=int(self.worker_settings.get("restart_timeout_seconds", 30)),
+            check=False,
+        )
+        return {
+            "status": "completed" if completed.returncode == 0 else "failed",
+            "returncode": completed.returncode,
+            "stdout": completed.stdout[-500:],
+            "stderr": completed.stderr[-500:],
+        }
+
+    def process(self, limit: int | None = None) -> dict[str, Any]:
+        queue = self._load_queue()
+        now_iso = _now().isoformat()
+        processed = []
+        pending_items = [item for item in queue.get("items", []) if item.get("status") == "pending"]
+        for index, item in enumerate(pending_items):
+            if limit is not None and index >= limit:
+                break
+            if item["action_type"] == "restart_agent":
+                result = self._restart_agent(item)
+            else:
+                result = self._apply_override(item, now_iso)
+            item["processed_at"] = now_iso
+            item["status"] = result["status"]
+            item["result"] = result
+            processed.append({"target": item.get("target"), "action_type": item["action_type"], **result})
+
+        queue["updated_at"] = now_iso
+        _write_json(self._resolve("recovery_queue_path"), queue)
+
+        refreshed_plan = self.harness.build_plan()
+        _write_json(self._resolve("output_plan_path"), refreshed_plan)
+        _write_json(self._resolve("runtime_state_path"), refreshed_plan["runtime"])
+
+        return {
+            "processed_count": len(processed),
+            "processed": processed,
+            "queue_size": len(queue.get("items", [])),
+        }
+
+
+def main() -> None:
+    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Consume autonomous recovery queue")
+    parser.add_argument("--limit", type=int, default=None, help="最多處理幾筆 pending item")
+    args = parser.parse_args()
+
+    worker = AutonomousRecoveryWorker()
+    result = worker.process(limit=args.limit)
+    print(json.dumps(result, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2))
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    main()

+# Agent Harness Self-Management Task
+
+## 目標
+- 深入研究目前專案使用的 agent harness。
+- 產出研究報告與優化方案，聚焦 self-healing 與 self-management。
+- 完成至少一項可驗證的自治能力實作，並補上測試。
+- 任務完成後通知 `wsngsc2025`。
+
+## 必用 Skill
+- `cursor-cli`
+- `knowledge-query`
+- `web-research`
+- `ntfy-notify`
+
+## 執行步驟
+1. 讀取 `skills/SKILL_INDEX.md` 與相關 `SKILL.md`。
+2. 確認目前 harness 版本、設計文件、原始碼與最新變更說明。
+3. 盤點現有自癒/自治能力與缺口。
+4. 產出 Markdown 研究報告與優化方案。
+5. 實作至少一項能強化自治閉環的功能，包含測試。
+6. 驗證測試與故障情境。
+7. 以 ntfy 通知 `wsngsc2025`。
+
+## 規則
+- 外部功能與 Skill 調用必須先實際執行。
+- 若 CLI、外部服務或通知失敗，需記錄 fallback 與失敗原因。
+- 所有產出與修改必須留在 `D:\Source\daily-digest-prompt`。
+
+## 最終回報格式
+- 以正體中文輸出。
+- 提供執行摘要、主要發現、知識庫、延伸方向。

diff --git a/tools/autonomous_recovery_worker.py b/tools/autonomous_recovery_worker.py
new file mode 100644
index 0000000000000000000000000000000000000000..d902134e8da32937aa25d6acd411f89d5e488045
--- /dev/null
+++ b/tools/autonomous_recovery_worker.py
@@ -0,0 +1,188 @@
+#!/usr/bin/env python3
+"""
+Autonomous recovery worker.
+
+消費 autonomous-recovery-queue，將控制面的恢復決策轉為可執行動作：
+- restart_agent: 執行安全的重啟命令
+- queue_self_heal / rebalance_tasks / scale_down_workload: 寫入暫時 runtime override
+"""
+from __future__ import annotations
+
+import argparse
+import json
+import subprocess
+from datetime import timedelta
+from pathlib import Path
+from typing import Any
+
+from tools.autonomous_harness import (
+    CONFIG_PATH,
+    REPO_ROOT,
+    AutonomousHarness,
+    _load_json,
+    _now,
+    _write_json,
+)
+
+
+class AutonomousRecoveryWorker:
+    def __init__(self, repo_root: Path | None = None, config_path: Path | None = None) -> None:
+        self.harness = AutonomousHarness(
+            repo_root=repo_root or REPO_ROOT,
+            config_path=config_path or CONFIG_PATH,
+        )
+        self.repo_root = self.harness.repo_root
+        self.settings = self.harness.settings
+        self.worker_settings = self.harness.recovery_worker
+
+    def _resolve(self, key: str) -> Path:
+        return self.repo_root / self.settings[key]
+
+    def _load_queue(self) -> dict[str, Any]:
+        return _load_json(self._resolve("recovery_queue_path"), {"version": 1, "items": []})
+
+    def _load_override(self) -> dict[str, Any]:
+        return _load_json(
+            self._resolve("runtime_override_path"),
+            {
+                "mode": None,
+                "reason": None,
+                "expires_at": None,
+                "blocked_task_keys": [],
+                "blocked_fetch_agents": [],
+            },
+        )
+
+    def _load_self_heal_requests(self) -> dict[str, Any]:
+        return _load_json(self._resolve("self_heal_request_path"), {"version": 1, "items": []})
+
+    def _write_override(self, override: dict[str, Any]) -> None:
+        _write_json(self._resolve("runtime_override_path"), override)
+
+    def _append_self_heal_request(self, target: str, reason: str, queued_at: str) -> None:
+        payload = self._load_self_heal_requests()
+        payload["items"].append(
+            {
+                "queued_at": queued_at,
+                "target": target,
+                "reason": reason,
+                "status": "pending",
+            }
+        )
+        payload["updated_at"] = queued_at
+        _write_json(self._resolve("self_heal_request_path"), payload)
+
+    def _apply_override(self, item: dict[str, Any], now_iso: str) -> dict[str, Any]:
+        override = self._load_override()
+        mode = "degraded"
+        ttl_minutes = int(self.worker_settings.get("default_override_ttl_minutes", 30))
+        blocked_task_keys = set(override.get("blocked_task_keys", []))
+        blocked_fetch_agents = set(override.get("blocked_fetch_agents", []))
+        max_parallel_auto_tasks = override.get("max_parallel_auto_tasks")
+        max_parallel_fetch_agents = override.get("max_parallel_fetch_agents")
+
+        if item["action_type"] == "scale_down_workload":
+            mode = "recovery" if item["severity"] == "critical" else "degraded"
+            ttl_minutes = int(self.worker_settings.get("scale_down_ttl_minutes", ttl_minutes))
+            max_parallel_auto_tasks = min(int(max_parallel_auto_tasks or 99), 1 if mode == "recovery" else 2)
+            max_parallel_fetch_agents = min(
+                int(max_parallel_fetch_agents or 99),
+                3 if mode == "recovery" else 4,
+            )
+        elif item["action_type"] == "rebalance_tasks":
+            ttl_minutes = int(self.worker_settings.get("rebalance_ttl_minutes", ttl_minutes))
+            max_parallel_auto_tasks = min(int(max_parallel_auto_tasks or 99), 2)
+        elif item["action_type"] == "queue_self_heal":
+            ttl_minutes = int(self.worker_settings.get("self_heal_ttl_minutes", ttl_minutes))
+            mode = "degraded"
+            target = item.get("target", "")
+            if target and target not in {"scheduler-heartbeat", "global"}:
+                blocked_task_keys.add(target)
+            if target in {"gmail", "security", "chatroom", "news", "todoist", "hackernews"}:
+                blocked_fetch_agents.add(target)
+            self._append_self_heal_request(target or "unknown", item["reason"], now_iso)
+
+        expires_at = (_now() + timedelta(minutes=ttl_minutes)).isoformat()
+        override.update(
+            {
+                "mode": mode,
+                "reason": item["reason"],
+                "expires_at": expires_at,
+                "blocked_task_keys": sorted(blocked_task_keys),
+                "blocked_fetch_agents": sorted(blocked_fetch_agents),
+            }
+        )
+        if max_parallel_auto_tasks is not None:
+            override["max_parallel_auto_tasks"] = max_parallel_auto_tasks
+        if max_parallel_fetch_agents is not None:
+            override["max_parallel_fetch_agents"] = max_parallel_fetch_agents
+        self._write_override(override)
+        return {"status": "completed", "effect": "runtime_override_updated", "expires_at": expires_at}
+
+    def _restart_agent(self, item: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
+        command = item.get("command")
+        if not command:
+            dispatch = self.harness.dispatch.get(item.get("target", ""), {})
+            command = dispatch.get("restart_command")
+        if not command:
+            return {"status": "failed", "error": "missing_restart_command"}
+
+        completed = subprocess.run(
+            command,
+            cwd=self.repo_root,
+            capture_output=True,
+            text=True,
+            encoding="utf-8",
+            timeout=int(self.worker_settings.get("restart_timeout_seconds", 30)),
+            check=False,
+        )
+        return {
+            "status": "completed" if completed.returncode == 0 else "failed",
+            "returncode": completed.returncode,
+            "stdout": completed.stdout[-500:],
+            "stderr": completed.stderr[-500:],
+        }
+
+    def process(self, limit: int | None = None) -> dict[str, Any]:
+        queue = self._load_queue()
+        now_iso = _now().isoformat()
+        processed = []
+        pending_items = [item for item in queue.get("items", []) if item.get("status") == "pending"]
+        for index, item in enumerate(pending_items):
+            if limit is not None and index >= limit:
+                break
+            if item["action_type"] == "restart_agent":
+                result = self._restart_agent(item)
+            else:
+                result = self._apply_override(item, now_iso)
+            item["processed_at"] = now_iso
+            item["status"] = result["status"]
+            item["result"] = result
+            processed.append({"target": item.get("target"), "action_type": item["action_type"], **result})
+
+        queue["updated_at"] = now_iso
+        _write_json(self._resolve("recovery_queue_path"), queue)
+
+        refreshed_plan = self.harness.build_plan()
+        _write_json(self._resolve("output_plan_path"), refreshed_plan)
+        _write_json(self._resolve("runtime_state_path"), refreshed_plan["runtime"])
+
+        return {
+            "processed_count": len(processed),
+            "processed": processed,
+            "queue_size": len(queue.get("items", [])),
+        }
+
+
+def main() -> None:
+    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Consume autonomous recovery queue")
+    parser.add_argument("--limit", type=int, default=None, help="最多處理幾筆 pending item")
+    args = parser.parse_args()
+
+    worker = AutonomousRecoveryWorker()
+    result = worker.process(limit=args.limit)
+    print(json.dumps(result, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2))
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    main()

diff --git a/tools/autonomous_recovery_worker.py b/tools/autonomous_recovery_worker.py
new file mode 100644
index 0000000000000000000000000000000000000000..d902134e8da32937aa25d6acd411f89d5e488045
--- /dev/null
+++ b/tools/autonomous_recovery_worker.py
@@ -0,0 +1,188 @@
+#!/usr/bin/env python3
+"""
+Autonomous recovery worker.
+
+消費 autonomous-recovery-queue，將控制面的恢復決策轉為可執行動作：
+- restart_agent: 執行安全的重啟命令
+- queue_self_heal / rebalance_tasks / scale_down_workload: 寫入暫時 runtime override
+"""
+from __future__ import annotations
+
+import argparse
+import json
+import subprocess
+from datetime import timedelta
+from pathlib import Path
+from typing import Any
+
+from tools.autonomous_harness import (
+    CONFIG_PATH,
+    REPO_ROOT,
+    AutonomousHarness,
+    _load_json,
+    _now,
+    _write_json,
+)
+
+
+class AutonomousRecoveryWorker:
+    def __init__(self, repo_root: Path | None = None, config_path: Path | None = None) -> None:
+        self.harness = AutonomousHarness(
+            repo_root=repo_root or REPO_ROOT,
+            config_path=config_path or CONFIG_PATH,
+        )
+        self.repo_root = self.harness.repo_root
+        self.settings = self.harness.settings
+        self.worker_settings = self.harness.recovery_worker
+
+    def _resolve(self, key: str) -> Path:
+        return self.repo_root / self.settings[key]
+
+    def _load_queue(self) -> dict[str, Any]:
+        return _load_json(self._resolve("recovery_queue_path"), {"version": 1, "items": []})
+
+    def _load_override(self) -> dict[str, Any]:
+        return _load_json(
+            self._resolve("runtime_override_path"),
+            {
+                "mode": None,
+                "reason": None,
+                "expires_at": None,
+                "blocked_task_keys": [],
+                "blocked_fetch_agents": [],
+            },
+        )
+
+    def _load_self_heal_requests(self) -> dict[str, Any]:
+        return _load_json(self._resolve("self_heal_request_path"), {"version": 1, "items": []})
+
+    def _write_override(self, override: dict[str, Any]) -> None:
+        _write_json(self._resolve("runtime_override_path"), override)
+
+    def _append_self_heal_request(self, target: str, reason: str, queued_at: str) -> None:
+        payload = self._load_self_heal_requests()
+        payload["items"].append(
+            {
+                "queued_at": queued_at,
+                "target": target,
+                "reason": reason,
+                "status": "pending",
+            }
+        )
+        payload["updated_at"] = queued_at
+        _write_json(self._resolve("self_heal_request_path"), payload)
+
+    def _apply_override(self, item: dict[str, Any], now_iso: str) -> dict[str, Any]:
+        override = self._load_override()
+        mode = "degraded"
+        ttl_minutes = int(self.worker_settings.get("default_override_ttl_minutes", 30))
+        blocked_task_keys = set(override.get("blocked_task_keys", []))
+        blocked_fetch_agents = set(override.get("blocked_fetch_agents", []))
+        max_parallel_auto_tasks = override.get("max_parallel_auto_tasks")
+        max_parallel_fetch_agents = override.get("max_parallel_fetch_agents")
+
+        if item["action_type"] == "scale_down_workload":
+            mode = "recovery" if item["severity"] == "critical" else "degraded"
+            ttl_minutes = int(self.worker_settings.get("scale_down_ttl_minutes", ttl_minutes))
+            max_parallel_auto_tasks = min(int(max_parallel_auto_tasks or 99), 1 if mode == "recovery" else 2)
+            max_parallel_fetch_agents = min(
+                int(max_parallel_fetch_agents or 99),
+                3 if mode == "recovery" else 4,
+            )
+        elif item["action_type"] == "rebalance_tasks":
+            ttl_minutes = int(self.worker_settings.get("rebalance_ttl_minutes", ttl_minutes))
+            max_parallel_auto_tasks = min(int(max_parallel_auto_tasks or 99), 2)
+        elif item["action_type"] == "queue_self_heal":
+            ttl_minutes = int(self.worker_settings.get("self_heal_ttl_minutes", ttl_minutes))
+            mode = "degraded"
+            target = item.get("target", "")
+            if target and target not in {"scheduler-heartbeat", "global"}:
+                blocked_task_keys.add(target)
+            if target in {"gmail", "security", "chatroom", "news", "todoist", "hackernews"}:
+                blocked_fetch_agents.add(target)
+            self._append_self_heal_request(target or "unknown", item["reason"], now_iso)
+
+        expires_at = (_now() + timedelta(minutes=ttl_minutes)).isoformat()
+        override.update(
+            {
+                "mode": mode,
+                "reason": item["reason"],
+                "expires_at": expires_at,
+                "blocked_task_keys": sorted(blocked_task_keys),
+                "blocked_fetch_agents": sorted(blocked_fetch_agents),
+            }
+        )
+        if max_parallel_auto_tasks is not None:
+            override["max_parallel_auto_tasks"] = max_parallel_auto_tasks
+        if max_parallel_fetch_agents is not None:
+            override["max_parallel_fetch_agents"] = max_parallel_fetch_agents
+        self._write_override(override)
+        return {"status": "completed", "effect": "runtime_override_updated", "expires_at": expires_at}
+
+    def _restart_agent(self, item: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
+        command = item.get("command")
+        if not command:
+            dispatch = self.harness.dispatch.get(item.get("target", ""), {})
+            command = dispatch.get("restart_command")
+        if not command:
+            return {"status": "failed", "error": "missing_restart_command"}
+
+        completed = subprocess.run(
+            command,
+            cwd=self.repo_root,
+            capture_output=True,
+            text=True,
+            encoding="utf-8",
+            timeout=int(self.worker_settings.get("restart_timeout_seconds", 30)),
+            check=False,
+        )
+        return {
+            "status": "completed" if completed.returncode == 0 else "failed",
+            "returncode": completed.returncode,
+            "stdout": completed.stdout[-500:],
+            "stderr": completed.stderr[-500:],
+        }
+
+    def process(self, limit: int | None = None) -> dict[str, Any]:
+        queue = self._load_queue()
+        now_iso = _now().isoformat()
+        processed = []
+        pending_items = [item for item in queue.get("items", []) if item.get("status") == "pending"]
+        for index, item in enumerate(pending_items):
+            if limit is not None and index >= limit:
+                break
+            if item["action_type"] == "restart_agent":
+                result = self._restart_agent(item)
+            else:
+                result = self._apply_override(item, now_iso)
+            item["processed_at"] = now_iso
+            item["status"] = result["status"]
+            item["result"] = result
+            processed.append({"target": item.get("target"), "action_type": item["action_type"], **result})
+
+        queue["updated_at"] = now_iso
+        _write_json(self._resolve("recovery_queue_path"), queue)
+
+        refreshed_plan = self.harness.build_plan()
+        _write_json(self._resolve("output_plan_path"), refreshed_plan)
+        _write_json(self._resolve("runtime_state_path"), refreshed_plan["runtime"])
+
+        return {
+            "processed_count": len(processed),
+            "processed": processed,
+            "queue_size": len(queue.get("items", [])),
+        }
+
+
+def main() -> None:
+    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Consume autonomous recovery queue")
+    parser.add_argument("--limit", type=int, default=None, help="最多處理幾筆 pending item")
+    args = parser.parse_args()
+
+    worker = AutonomousRecoveryWorker()
+    result = worker.process(limit=args.limit)
+    print(json.dumps(result, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2))
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    main()

+# Agent Harness Self-Management Task
+
+## 目標
+- 深入研究目前專案使用的 agent harness。
+- 產出研究報告與優化方案，聚焦 self-healing 與 self-management。
+- 完成至少一項可驗證的自治能力實作，並補上測試。
+- 任務完成後通知 `wsngsc2025`。
+
+## 必用 Skill
+- `cursor-cli`
+- `knowledge-query`
+- `web-research`
+- `ntfy-notify`
+
+## 執行步驟
+1. 讀取 `skills/SKILL_INDEX.md` 與相關 `SKILL.md`。
+2. 確認目前 harness 版本、設計文件、原始碼與最新變更說明。
+3. 盤點現有自癒/自治能力與缺口。
+4. 產出 Markdown 研究報告與優化方案。
+5. 實作至少一項能強化自治閉環的功能，包含測試。
+6. 驗證測試與故障情境。
+7. 以 ntfy 通知 `wsngsc2025`。
+
+## 規則
+- 外部功能與 Skill 調用必須先實際執行。
+- 若 CLI、外部服務或通知失敗，需記錄 fallback 與失敗原因。
+- 所有產出與修改必須留在 `D:\Source\daily-digest-prompt`。
+
+## 最終回報格式
+- 以正體中文輸出。
+- 提供執行摘要、主要發現、知識庫、延伸方向。

+#!/usr/bin/env python3
+"""
+Autonomous recovery worker.
+
+消費 autonomous-recovery-queue，將控制面的恢復決策轉為可執行動作：
+- restart_agent: 執行安全的重啟命令
+- queue_self_heal / rebalance_tasks / scale_down_workload: 寫入暫時 runtime override
+"""
+from __future__ import annotations
+
+import argparse
+import json
+import subprocess
+from datetime import timedelta
+from pathlib import Path
+from typing import Any
+
+from tools.autonomous_harness import (
+    CONFIG_PATH,
+    REPO_ROOT,
+    AutonomousHarness,
+    _load_json,
+    _now,
+    _write_json,
+)
+
+
+class AutonomousRecoveryWorker:
+    def __init__(self, repo_root: Path | None = None, config_path: Path | None = None) -> None:
+        self.harness = AutonomousHarness(
+            repo_root=repo_root or REPO_ROOT,
+            config_path=config_path or CONFIG_PATH,
+        )
+        self.repo_root = self.harness.repo_root
+        self.settings = self.harness.settings
+        self.worker_settings = self.harness.recovery_worker
+
+    def _resolve(self, key: str) -> Path:
+        return self.repo_root / self.settings[key]
+
+    def _load_queue(self) -> dict[str, Any]:
+        return _load_json(self._resolve("recovery_queue_path"), {"version": 1, "items": []})
+
+    def _load_override(self) -> dict[str, Any]:
+        return _load_json(
+            self._resolve("runtime_override_path"),
+            {
+                "mode": None,
+                "reason": None,
+                "expires_at": None,
+                "blocked_task_keys": [],
+                "blocked_fetch_agents": [],
+            },
+        )
+
+    def _load_self_heal_requests(self) -> dict[str, Any]:
+        return _load_json(self._resolve("self_heal_request_path"), {"version": 1, "items": []})
+
+    def _write_override(self, override: dict[str, Any]) -> None:
+        _write_json(self._resolve("runtime_override_path"), override)
+
+    def _append_self_heal_request(self, target: str, reason: str, queued_at: str) -> None:
+        payload = self._load_self_heal_requests()
+        payload["items"].append(
+            {
+                "queued_at": queued_at,
+                "target": target,
+                "reason": reason,
+                "status": "pending",
+            }
+        )
+        payload["updated_at"] = queued_at
+        _write_json(self._resolve("self_heal_request_path"), payload)
+
+    def _apply_override(self, item: dict[str, Any], now_iso: str) -> dict[str, Any]:
+        override = self._load_override()
+        mode = "degraded"
+        ttl_minutes = int(self.worker_settings.get("default_override_ttl_minutes", 30))
+        blocked_task_keys = set(override.get("blocked_task_keys", []))
+        blocked_fetch_agents = set(override.get("blocked_fetch_agents", []))
+        max_parallel_auto_tasks = override.get("max_parallel_auto_tasks")
+        max_parallel_fetch_agents = override.get("max_parallel_fetch_agents")
+
+        if item["action_type"] == "scale_down_workload":
+            mode = "recovery" if item["severity"] == "critical" else "degraded"
+            ttl_minutes = int(self.worker_settings.get("scale_down_ttl_minutes", ttl_minutes))
+            max_parallel_auto_tasks = min(int(max_parallel_auto_tasks or 99), 1 if mode == "recovery" else 2)
+            max_parallel_fetch_agents = min(
+                int(max_parallel_fetch_agents or 99),
+                3 if mode == "recovery" else 4,
+            )
+        elif item["action_type"] == "rebalance_tasks":
+            ttl_minutes = int(self.worker_settings.get("rebalance_ttl_minutes", ttl_minutes))
+            max_parallel_auto_tasks = min(int(max_parallel_auto_tasks or 99), 2)
+        elif item["action_type"] == "queue_self_heal":
+            ttl_minutes = int(self.worker_settings.get("self_heal_ttl_minutes", ttl_minutes))
+            mode = "degraded"
+            target = item.get("target", "")
+            if target and target not in {"scheduler-heartbeat", "global"}:
+                blocked_task_keys.add(target)
+            if target in {"gmail", "security", "chatroom", "news", "todoist", "hackernews"}:
+                blocked_fetch_agents.add(target)
+            self._append_self_heal_request(target or "unknown", item["reason"], now_iso)
+
+        expires_at = (_now() + timedelta(minutes=ttl_minutes)).isoformat()
+        override.update(
+            {
+                "mode": mode,
+                "reason": item["reason"],
+                "expires_at": expires_at,
+                "blocked_task_keys": sorted(blocked_task_keys),
+                "blocked_fetch_agents": sorted(blocked_fetch_agents),
+            }
+        )
+        if max_parallel_auto_tasks is not None:
+            override["max_parallel_auto_tasks"] = max_parallel_auto_tasks
+        if max_parallel_fetch_agents is not None:
+            override["max_parallel_fetch_agents"] = max_parallel_fetch_agents
+        self._write_override(override)
+        return {"status": "completed", "effect": "runtime_override_updated", "expires_at": expires_at}
+
+    def _restart_agent(self, item: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
+        command = item.get("command")
+        if not command:
+            dispatch = self.harness.dispatch.get(item.get("target", ""), {})
+            command = dispatch.get("restart_command")
+        if not command:
+            return {"status": "failed", "error": "missing_restart_command"}
+
+        completed = subprocess.run(
+            command,
+            cwd=self.repo_root,
+            capture_output=True,
+            text=True,
+            encoding="utf-8",
+            timeout=int(self.worker_settings.get("restart_timeout_seconds", 30)),
+            check=False,
+        )
+        return {
+            "status": "completed" if completed.returncode == 0 else "failed",
+            "returncode": completed.returncode,
+            "stdout": completed.stdout[-500:],
+            "stderr": completed.stderr[-500:],
+        }
+
+    def process(self, limit: int | None = None) -> dict[str, Any]:
+        queue = self._load_queue()
+        now_iso = _now().isoformat()
+        processed = []
+        pending_items = [item for item in queue.get("items", []) if item.get("status") == "pending"]
+        for index, item in enumerate(pending_items):
+            if limit is not None and index >= limit:
+                break
+            if item["action_type"] == "restart_agent":
+                result = self._restart_agent(item)
+            else:
+                result = self._apply_override(item, now_iso)
+            item["processed_at"] = now_iso
+            item["status"] = result["status"]
+            item["result"] = result
+            processed.append({"target": item.get("target"), "action_type": item["action_type"], **result})
+
+        queue["updated_at"] = now_iso
+        _write_json(self._resolve("recovery_queue_path"), queue)
+
+        refreshed_plan = self.harness.build_plan()
+        _write_json(self._resolve("output_plan_path"), refreshed_plan)
+        _write_json(self._resolve("runtime_state_path"), refreshed_plan["runtime"])
+
+        return {
+            "processed_count": len(processed),
+            "processed": processed,
+            "queue_size": len(queue.get("items", [])),
+        }
+
+
+def main() -> None:
+    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Consume autonomous recovery queue")
+    parser.add_argument("--limit", type=int, default=None, help="最多處理幾筆 pending item")
+    args = parser.parse_args()
+
+    worker = AutonomousRecoveryWorker()
+    result = worker.process(limit=args.limit)
+    print(json.dumps(result, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2))
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    main()

+# Agent Harness Self-Management Task
+
+## 目標
+- 深入研究目前專案使用的 agent harness。
+- 產出研究報告與優化方案，聚焦 self-healing 與 self-management。
+- 完成至少一項可驗證的自治能力實作，並補上測試。
+- 任務完成後通知 `wsngsc2025`。
+
+## 必用 Skill
+- `cursor-cli`
+- `knowledge-query`
+- `web-research`
+- `ntfy-notify`
+
+## 執行步驟
+1. 讀取 `skills/SKILL_INDEX.md` 與相關 `SKILL.md`。
+2. 確認目前 harness 版本、設計文件、原始碼與最新變更說明。
+3. 盤點現有自癒/自治能力與缺口。
+4. 產出 Markdown 研究報告與優化方案。
+5. 實作至少一項能強化自治閉環的功能，包含測試。
+6. 驗證測試與故障情境。
+7. 以 ntfy 通知 `wsngsc2025`。
+
+## 規則
+- 外部功能與 Skill 調用必須先實際執行。
+- 若 CLI、外部服務或通知失敗，需記錄 fallback 與失敗原因。
+- 所有產出與修改必須留在 `D:\Source\daily-digest-prompt`。
+
+## 最終回報格式
+- 以正體中文輸出。
+- 提供執行摘要、主要發現、知識庫、延伸方向。

+#!/usr/bin/env python3
+"""
+Autonomous recovery worker.
+
+消費 autonomous-recovery-queue，將控制面的恢復決策轉為可執行動作：
+- restart_agent: 執行安全的重啟命令
+- queue_self_heal / rebalance_tasks / scale_down_workload: 寫入暫時 runtime override
+"""
+from __future__ import annotations
+
+import argparse
+import json
+import subprocess
+from datetime import timedelta
+from pathlib import Path
+from typing import Any
+
+from tools.autonomous_harness import (
+    CONFIG_PATH,
+    REPO_ROOT,
+    AutonomousHarness,
+    _load_json,
+    _now,
+    _write_json,
+)
+
+
+class AutonomousRecoveryWorker:
+    def __init__(self, repo_root: Path | None = None, config_path: Path | None = None) -> None:
+        self.harness = AutonomousHarness(
+            repo_root=repo_root or REPO_ROOT,
+            config_path=config_path or CONFIG_PATH,
+        )
+        self.repo_root = self.harness.repo_root
+        self.settings = self.harness.settings
+        self.worker_settings = self.harness.recovery_worker
+
+    def _resolve(self, key: str) -> Path:
+        return self.repo_root / self.settings[key]
+
+    def _load_queue(self) -> dict[str, Any]:
+        return _load_json(self._resolve("recovery_queue_path"), {"version": 1, "items": []})
+
+    def _load_override(self) -> dict[str, Any]:
+        return _load_json(
+            self._resolve("runtime_override_path"),
+            {
+                "mode": None,
+                "reason": None,
+                "expires_at": None,
+                "blocked_task_keys": [],
+                "blocked_fetch_agents": [],
+            },
+        )
+
+    def _load_self_heal_requests(self) -> dict[str, Any]:
+        return _load_json(self._resolve("self_heal_request_path"), {"version": 1, "items": []})
+
+    def _write_override(self, override: dict[str, Any]) -> None:
+        _write_json(self._resolve("runtime_override_path"), override)
+
+    def _append_self_heal_request(self, target: str, reason: str, queued_at: str) -> None:
+        payload = self._load_self_heal_requests()
+        payload["items"].append(
+            {
+                "queued_at": queued_at,
+                "target": target,
+                "reason": reason,
+                "status": "pending",
+            }
+        )
+        payload["updated_at"] = queued_at
+        _write_json(self._resolve("self_heal_request_path"), payload)
+
+    def _apply_override(self, item: dict[str, Any], now_iso: str) -> dict[str, Any]:
+        override = self._load_override()
+        mode = "degraded"
+        ttl_minutes = int(self.worker_settings.get("default_override_ttl_minutes", 30))
+        blocked_task_keys = set(override.get("blocked_task_keys", []))
+        blocked_fetch_agents = set(override.get("blocked_fetch_agents", []))
+        max_parallel_auto_tasks = override.get("max_parallel_auto_tasks")
+        max_parallel_fetch_agents = override.get("max_parallel_fetch_agents")
+
+        if item["action_type"] == "scale_down_workload":
+            mode = "recovery" if item["severity"] == "critical" else "degraded"
+            ttl_minutes = int(self.worker_settings.get("scale_down_ttl_minutes", ttl_minutes))
+            max_parallel_auto_tasks = min(int(max_parallel_auto_tasks or 99), 1 if mode == "recovery" else 2)
+            max_parallel_fetch_agents = min(
+                int(max_parallel_fetch_agents or 99),
+                3 if mode == "recovery" else 4,
+            )
+        elif item["action_type"] == "rebalance_tasks":
+            ttl_minutes = int(self.worker_settings.get("rebalance_ttl_minutes", ttl_minutes))
+            max_parallel_auto_tasks = min(int(max_parallel_auto_tasks or 99), 2)
+        elif item["action_type"] == "queue_self_heal":
+            ttl_minutes = int(self.worker_settings.get("self_heal_ttl_minutes", ttl_minutes))
+            mode = "degraded"
+            target = item.get("target", "")
+            if target and target not in {"scheduler-heartbeat", "global"}:
+                blocked_task_keys.add(target)
+            if target in {"gmail", "security", "chatroom", "news", "todoist", "hackernews"}:
+                blocked_fetch_agents.add(target)
+            self._append_self_heal_request(target or "unknown", item["reason"], now_iso)
+
+        expires_at = (_now() + timedelta(minutes=ttl_minutes)).isoformat()
+        override.update(
+            {
+                "mode": mode,
+                "reason": item["reason"],
+                "expires_at": expires_at,
+                "blocked_task_keys": sorted(blocked_task_keys),
+                "blocked_fetch_agents": sorted(blocked_fetch_agents),
+            }
+        )
+        if max_parallel_auto_tasks is not None:
+            override["max_parallel_auto_tasks"] = max_parallel_auto_tasks
+        if max_parallel_fetch_agents is not None:
+            override["max_parallel_fetch_agents"] = max_parallel_fetch_agents
+        self._write_override(override)
+        return {"status": "completed", "effect": "runtime_override_updated", "expires_at": expires_at}
+
+    def _restart_agent(self, item: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
+        command = item.get("command")
+        if not command:
+            dispatch = self.harness.dispatch.get(item.get("target", ""), {})
+            command = dispatch.get("restart_command")
+        if not command:
+            return {"status": "failed", "error": "missing_restart_command"}
+
+        completed = subprocess.run(
+            command,
+            cwd=self.repo_root,
+            capture_output=True,
+            text=True,
+            encoding="utf-8",
+            timeout=int(self.worker_settings.get("restart_timeout_seconds", 30)),
+            check=False,
+        )
+        return {
+            "status": "completed" if completed.returncode == 0 else "failed",
+            "returncode": completed.returncode,
+            "stdout": completed.stdout[-500:],
+            "stderr": completed.stderr[-500:],
+        }
+
+    def process(self, limit: int | None = None) -> dict[str, Any]:
+        queue = self._load_queue()
+        now_iso = _now().isoformat()
+        processed = []
+        pending_items = [item for item in queue.get("items", []) if item.get("status") == "pending"]
+        for index, item in enumerate(pending_items):
+            if limit is not None and index >= limit:
+                break
+            if item["action_type"] == "restart_agent":
+                result = self._restart_agent(item)
+            else:
+                result = self._apply_override(item, now_iso)
+            item["processed_at"] = now_iso
+            item["status"] = result["status"]
+            item["result"] = result
+            processed.append({"target": item.get("target"), "action_type": item["action_type"], **result})
+
+        queue["updated_at"] = now_iso
+        _write_json(self._resolve("recovery_queue_path"), queue)
+
+        refreshed_plan = self.harness.build_plan()
+        _write_json(self._resolve("output_plan_path"), refreshed_plan)
+        _write_json(self._resolve("runtime_state_path"), refreshed_plan["runtime"])
+
+        return {
+            "processed_count": len(processed),
+            "processed": processed,
+            "queue_size": len(queue.get("items", [])),
+        }
+
+
+def main() -> None:
+    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Consume autonomous recovery queue")
+    parser.add_argument("--limit", type=int, default=None, help="最多處理幾筆 pending item")
+    args = parser.parse_args()
+
+    worker = AutonomousRecoveryWorker()
+    result = worker.process(limit=args.limit)
+    print(json.dumps(result, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2))
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    main()

+            "self_heal_request_path": "state/autonomous-self-heal-requests.json",
             "thresholds": {

+    _write_json(tmp_path / "state" / "scheduler-state.json", {"runs": []})
+    _write_json(tmp_path / "state" / "failure-stats.json", {"updated": "2026-03-20T07:00:00+08:00"})
+    _write_json(tmp_path / "state" / "failed-auto-tasks.json", {"entries": []})
+    _write_json(tmp_path / "state" / "api-health.json", {"apis": {}})
+    _write_json(tmp_path / "state" / "auto-task-fairness-hint.json", {"starvation_detected": False, "starvation_count": 0})
+    _write_json(tmp_path / "state" / "token-budget-state.json", {"last_alerted_date": "2026-03-19"})
+    _write_json(tmp_path / "state" / "scheduler-heartbeat.json", {"timestamp": "2026-03-20T07:00:00+08:00", "status": "running"})
+    _write_json(
+        tmp_path / "state" / "autonomous-runtime-overrides.json",
+        {

+            "expires_at": "2026-03-20T08:00:00+08:00",

+    assert plan["runtime"]["policies"]["max_parallel_fetch_agents"] == 2

+# Agent Harness Self-Management Task
+
+## 目標
+- 深入研究目前專案使用的 agent harness。
+- 產出研究報告與優化方案，聚焦 self-healing 與 self-management。
+- 完成至少一項可驗證的自治能力實作，並補上測試。
+- 任務完成後通知 `wsngsc2025`。
+
+## 必用 Skill
+- `cursor-cli`
+- `knowledge-query`
+- `web-research`
+- `ntfy-notify`
+
+## 執行步驟
+1. 讀取 `skills/SKILL_INDEX.md` 與相關 `SKILL.md`。
+2. 確認目前 harness 版本、設計文件、原始碼與最新變更說明。
+3. 盤點現有自癒/自治能力與缺口。
+4. 產出 Markdown 研究報告與優化方案。
+5. 實作至少一項能強化自治閉環的功能，包含測試。
+6. 驗證測試與故障情境。
+7. 以 ntfy 通知 `wsngsc2025`。
+
+## 規則
+- 外部功能與 Skill 調用必須先實際執行。
+- 若 CLI、外部服務或通知失敗，需記錄 fallback 與失敗原因。
+- 所有產出與修改必須留在 `D:\Source\daily-digest-prompt`。
+
+## 最終回報格式
+- 以正體中文輸出。
+- 提供執行摘要、主要發現、知識庫、延伸方向。

diff --git a/tools/autonomous_recovery_worker.py b/tools/autonomous_recovery_worker.py
new file mode 100644
index 0000000000000000000000000000000000000000..d902134e8da32937aa25d6acd411f89d5e488045
--- /dev/null
+++ b/tools/autonomous_recovery_worker.py
@@ -0,0 +1,188 @@
+#!/usr/bin/env python3
+"""
+Autonomous recovery worker.
+
+消費 autonomous-recovery-queue，將控制面的恢復決策轉為可執行動作：
+- restart_agent: 執行安全的重啟命令
+- queue_self_heal / rebalance_tasks / scale_down_workload: 寫入暫時 runtime override
+"""
+from __future__ import annotations
+
+import argparse
+import json
+import subprocess
+from datetime import timedelta
+from pathlib import Path
+from typing import Any
+
+from tools.autonomous_harness import (
+    CONFIG_PATH,
+    REPO_ROOT,
+    AutonomousHarness,
+    _load_json,
+    _now,
+    _write_json,
+)
+
+
+class AutonomousRecoveryWorker:
+    def __init__(self, repo_root: Path | None = None, config_path: Path | None = None) -> None:
+        self.harness = AutonomousHarness(
+            repo_root=repo_root or REPO_ROOT,
+            config_path=config_path or CONFIG_PATH,
+        )
+        self.repo_root = self.harness.repo_root
+        self.settings = self.harness.settings
+        self.worker_settings = self.harness.recovery_worker
+
+    def _resolve(self, key: str) -> Path:
+        return self.repo_root / self.settings[key]
+
+    def _load_queue(self) -> dict[str, Any]:
+        return _load_json(self._resolve("recovery_queue_path"), {"version": 1, "items": []})
+
+    def _load_override(self) -> dict[str, Any]:
+        return _load_json(
+            self._resolve("runtime_override_path"),
+            {
+                "mode": None,
+                "reason": None,
+                "expires_at": None,
+                "blocked_task_keys": [],
+                "blocked_fetch_agents": [],
+            },
+        )
+
+    def _load_self_heal_requests(self) -> dict[str, Any]:
+        return _load_json(self._resolve("self_heal_request_path"), {"version": 1, "items": []})
+
+    def _write_override(self, override: dict[str, Any]) -> None:
+        _write_json(self._resolve("runtime_override_path"), override)
+
+    def _append_self_heal_request(self, target: str, reason: str, queued_at: str) -> None:
+        payload = self._load_self_heal_requests()
+        payload["items"].append(
+            {
+                "queued_at": queued_at,
+                "target": target,
+                "reason": reason,
+                "status": "pending",
+            }
+        )
+        payload["updated_at"] = queued_at
+        _write_json(self._resolve("self_heal_request_path"), payload)
+
+    def _apply_override(self, item: dict[str, Any], now_iso: str) -> dict[str, Any]:
+        override = self._load_override()
+        mode = "degraded"
+        ttl_minutes = int(self.worker_settings.get("default_override_ttl_minutes", 30))
+        blocked_task_keys = set(override.get("blocked_task_keys", []))
+        blocked_fetch_agents = set(override.get("blocked_fetch_agents", []))
+        max_parallel_auto_tasks = override.get("max_parallel_auto_tasks")
+        max_parallel_fetch_agents = override.get("max_parallel_fetch_agents")
+
+        if item["action_type"] == "scale_down_workload":
+            mode = "recovery" if item["severity"] == "critical" else "degraded"
+            ttl_minutes = int(self.worker_settings.get("scale_down_ttl_minutes", ttl_minutes))
+            max_parallel_auto_tasks = min(int(max_parallel_auto_tasks or 99), 1 if mode == "recovery" else 2)
+            max_parallel_fetch_agents = min(
+                int(max_parallel_fetch_agents or 99),
+                3 if mode == "recovery" else 4,
+            )
+        elif item["action_type"] == "rebalance_tasks":
+            ttl_minutes = int(self.worker_settings.get("rebalance_ttl_minutes", ttl_minutes))
+            max_parallel_auto_tasks = min(int(max_parallel_auto_tasks or 99), 2)
+        elif item["action_type"] == "queue_self_heal":
+            ttl_minutes = int(self.worker_settings.get("self_heal_ttl_minutes", ttl_minutes))
+            mode = "degraded"
+            target = item.get("target", "")
+            if target and target not in {"scheduler-heartbeat", "global"}:
+                blocked_task_keys.add(target)
+            if target in {"gmail", "security", "chatroom", "news", "todoist", "hackernews"}:
+                blocked_fetch_agents.add(target)
+            self._append_self_heal_request(target or "unknown", item["reason"], now_iso)
+
+        expires_at = (_now() + timedelta(minutes=ttl_minutes)).isoformat()
+        override.update(
+            {
+                "mode": mode,
+                "reason": item["reason"],
+                "expires_at": expires_at,
+                "blocked_task_keys": sorted(blocked_task_keys),
+                "blocked_fetch_agents": sorted(blocked_fetch_agents),
+            }
+        )
+        if max_parallel_auto_tasks is not None:
+            override["max_parallel_auto_tasks"] = max_parallel_auto_tasks
+        if max_parallel_fetch_agents is not None:
+            override["max_parallel_fetch_agents"] = max_parallel_fetch_agents
+        self._write_override(override)
+        return {"status": "completed", "effect": "runtime_override_updated", "expires_at": expires_at}
+
+    def _restart_agent(self, item: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
+        command = item.get("command")
+        if not command:
+            dispatch = self.harness.dispatch.get(item.get("target", ""), {})
+            command = dispatch.get("restart_command")
+        if not command:
+            return {"status": "failed", "error": "missing_restart_command"}
+
+        completed = subprocess.run(
+            command,
+            cwd=self.repo_root,
+            capture_output=True,
+            text=True,
+            encoding="utf-8",
+            timeout=int(self.worker_settings.get("restart_timeout_seconds", 30)),
+            check=False,
+        )
+        return {
+            "status": "completed" if completed.returncode == 0 else "failed",
+            "returncode": completed.returncode,
+            "stdout": completed.stdout[-500:],
+            "stderr": completed.stderr[-500:],
+        }
+
+    def process(self, limit: int | None = None) -> dict[str, Any]:
+        queue = self._load_queue()
+        now_iso = _now().isoformat()
+        processed = []
+        pending_items = [item for item in queue.get("items", []) if item.get("status") == "pending"]
+        for index, item in enumerate(pending_items):
+            if limit is not None and index >= limit:
+                break
+            if item["action_type"] == "restart_agent":
+                result = self._restart_agent(item)
+            else:
+                result = self._apply_override(item, now_iso)
+            item["processed_at"] = now_iso
+            item["status"] = result["status"]
+            item["result"] = result
+            processed.append({"target": item.get("target"), "action_type": item["action_type"], **result})
+
+        queue["updated_at"] = now_iso
+        _write_json(self._resolve("recovery_queue_path"), queue)
+
+        refreshed_plan = self.harness.build_plan()
+        _write_json(self._resolve("output_plan_path"), refreshed_plan)
+        _write_json(self._resolve("runtime_state_path"), refreshed_plan["runtime"])
+
+        return {
+            "processed_count": len(processed),
+            "processed": processed,
+            "queue_size": len(queue.get("items", [])),
+        }
+
+
+def main() -> None:
+    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Consume autonomous recovery queue")
+    parser.add_argument("--limit", type=int, default=None, help="最多處理幾筆 pending item")
+    args = parser.parse_args()
+
+    worker = AutonomousRecoveryWorker()
+    result = worker.process(limit=args.limit)
+    print(json.dumps(result, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2))
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    main()

   recovery_queue_path: "state/autonomous-recovery-queue.json"
   runtime_state_path: "state/autonomous-runtime.json"
+  runtime_override_path: "state/autonomous-runtime-overrides.json"
   agent_registry_path: "state/autonomous-agent-registry.json"
   resource_snapshot_path: "state/autonomous-resource-snapshot.json"
+  self_heal_request_path: "state/autonomous-self-heal-requests.json"

+    default_override_ttl_minutes: 30
+    scale_down_ttl_minutes: 45
+    rebalance_ttl_minutes: 30
+    self_heal_ttl_minutes: 60
+

     normal:
       max_parallel_auto_tasks: 4

+## 目標

+- 產出研究報告與優化方案，聚焦 self-healing 與 self-management。

+## 必用 Skill

+- `knowledge-query`
+- `web-research`
+- `ntfy-notify`
+
+## 執行步驟

+6. 驗證測試與故障情境。
+7. 以 ntfy 通知 `wsngsc2025`。

+
+## 最終回報格式
+- 以正體中文輸出。
+- 提供執行摘要、主要發現、知識庫、延伸方向。
